msg:The Banyan Tree Hotel, located in Nanjing Garden Expo Park, opened in 2021. It was built on the wall of an abandoned limestone mine to create a spectacular scene of a mist waterfall pouring down from the top of the cliff. The hotel is a resort hotel that combines beautiful scenery, food, and entertainment. Each room has a viewing balcony and an independent private hot spring pool. There is also a sky garden on the top floor. The scenery is spectacular and beautiful, and a casual shot is a blockbuster. The hotel also has travel photography services. I made an appointment with the hotel's travel photographer, Aze, who is very attentive in taking pictures. The one-stop travel photography took me around the hotel for shooting. The service was very good, and the front desk lady Molly was also very nice, enthusiastic and patient. The experience was good, recommended!

I will still choose to stay, for the soup house, I hope the details can be better. Next time I want to experience hotel dining.

Fix respawn thinking.
Service: Very attentive, the staff will greet each other when they see it, Grace, the front desk supervisor, will contact you in advance, the service is very thoughtful and the attitude is very good.
The hotel lobby is located on the eighth floor, and the unique cocoon-shaped installation is eye-catching. The half-enclosed shape is more like the moment of breaking out of the cocoon, exuding different charms whether it is day or night. In the lobby lounge with a wide view, one side is a cliff imitating the outdoor natural landscape, and the other side is surrounded by 180-degree floor-to-ceiling glass windows. Take a panoramic view of the cliff landscape and the wonders of the underwater botanical garden. When the sun sets, order an afternoon tea and watch the sunset quietly
All the rooms can see the beautiful scenery of the mine valley. The area is very large, mainly in black and log colors that resemble ore. There are aroma burners and incense inserts on the table, and there is a private hot spring pool on the balcony. Very good staying experience, will come again next time

üìçLocation environment

The hotel is built on the cliff‚õ∞Ô∏è, and the landform with a slight sense of technology is carefully designed to create a sense of design. The environment is like a secret mining valley.
.

.

.
The lobby lounge with a wide view, one side is a cliff imitating the outdoor natural landscape ‚õ∞Ô∏è The other side is surrounded by 180-degree floor-to-ceiling glass windows ü™ü You can have a panoramic view of the cliff landscape and the wonders of the underwater botanical garden. In the guest room, the green walls in the room also have obvious traces of wiping, and the pools are also full of white deposits from the hot springs. The waiter said that the soft drinks and beer in the MINI Bar are free. We drank two juices and wanted the waiter to add more. Two bottles, was told there is a charge for refills.
If the room fee is 1,000 yuan, these are not problems, but it is difficult for people to accept such a service with a room fee of more than 5,000 yuan. Just took some pictures of the dirty hotel.
